It turns your Windows device with a camera into a handy scanner, suitable for scanning various documents like contracts, articles, business cards, notes, receipts, warranty papers etc. Image capture is done with the help of Real-Time Edge Detection (auto crop).\r\n\r\nThis scanner app also excels in import options. It imports variety of document formats, such as odt, ods, odp, csv, svg, hwp and many others.
